It will initiate the revitalization of Cauvery river and transform the lives of 84 million people.\n\nCauvery Calling will support farmers to plant 242 crore trees in Cauvery basin by shifting to agroforestry, with 73 crore trees in the first phase across Tamil Nadu and Karnataka. \n\nRiver Cauvery and its basin has been one of the most productive basins in the world. But today its water flow has shrunk by over 40% in 70 years. In 2016, the Kaveri went dry at its source as rainfall fell by 40-70%. Ironically, Tamil Nadu had suffered some of its worst floods a few months earlier in 2015. Five hundred people lost their lives. Estimates of the damage ranged from INR 20,000-160,000 crores. And a year later in the summer of 2017, once again, Tamil Nadu faced drought – the worst in 140 years, while Karnataka stares at a 36% shortfall in food grain production. Organic Thinking of Preservation and legacy of culture and Heritage of Ponca Nations\n\nWhat does SHADES OF RED mean?  SHADES could mean the organic journey of the Native people since their existence started to today and into the future. The Natives have experienced genocide, racism, stereotype, exploitation, as well as unsettled future in tribal sovereignty and federal policy, it is good to see another Shade of Red is emerging – more educated and more prideful Indians standing up.\n\nAmerican Indian IDENTITY is most important because it gives the Native a sense of belonging, whether it was imposed by the coloring of skin, or by the federal government; however, it also means we are the only race that has to provide document to prove tribal identification\n\nThe 2019 AIHD Profile in History will feature the Ponca Tribe of Oklahoma and the Ponca Tribe of Nebraska. The most important leader is Chief Standing Bear.  Why are we not all familiar with his accomplishment?  Standing Bear was a Ponca chief and Native American civil rights leader who successfully argued in U.S. District Court in 1879 in Omaha that Native Americans are “persons within the meaning of the law” and have the right of habeas corpus, thus becoming the first Native American judicially granted civil rights under American law.  \n\nOne of the most important Shade of Red in the preservation and legacy of culture and heritage is dialect and being protectors of our murdered and missing Indian women and boys of all classes.\n\nOur life as we learn, educate, and teach the right way through भी बुरा प्रभाव देने लगती है। इससे श्वास रोग, वायु विकार, फेफड़ों में दर्द आदि होने लगता है। कुंडली में गुरु-शनि, गुरु-राहु और गुरु-बुध जब मिलते हैं तो अस्थमा, दमा, श्वास आदि के रोग, गर्दन, नाक या सिर में दर्द भी होने लगता है। इसके अलावा गुरु की राहु, शनि और बुध के साथ युति अनुसार भी बीमारियां होती हैं, जैसे- पेचिश, रीढ़ की हड्डी में दर्द, कब्ज, रक्त विकार, कानदर्द, पेट फूलना, जिगर में खराबी आदि।
